  rem   standby 0    Destination for standby command = 0 (TV)
  rem   COM2    COM port on PC = 2
  rem   -t r    Type of device to emulate = Recording Device (includes Playback Device functionality)
  rem   -p 1    Port on TV to use as active source = HDMI1
  rem   -b 0    Base (logical address) of TV = 0
  rem   -d 1    Debug level = 1 (show errors only)
  rem   -s      Single command execute, then exit

рдпрджрд┐ рдЖрдк рдореЙрдирд┐рдЯрд░ рдХреЛ рдЪрд╛рд▓реВ рдХрд░рддреЗ рд╣реИрдВ рдЬрдм рдХрдВрдкреНрдпреВрдЯрд░ рд╕реНрд▓реАрдк рдпрд╛ рд╣рд╛рдЗрдмрд░рдиреЗрдЯ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд┐ рдореЗрдВ рд╣реЛрддрд╛ рд╣реИ, рддреЛ рдкреАрд╕реА рдЪрд╛рд▓реВ рд╣реЛрддрд╛ рд╣реИред

рд╕рднреА рдХрдорд┐рдпреЛрдВ рдХреЗ рдмрд╛рд╡рдЬреВрдж, рдореБрдЭреЗ рдПрдбреЙрдкреНрдЯрд░ рдХрд╛ рдЕрдиреБрднрд╡ рдФрд░ рдЕрдВрддрд┐рдо рдкрд░рд┐рдгрд╛рдо рдЗрддрдирд╛ рдкрд╕рдВрдж рдЖрдпрд╛ рдХрд┐ рдореИрдВрдиреЗ рдЕрдореЗрдЬрд╝рди рдкрд░ рдЗрд╕рдХреЗ рдмрд╛рд░реЗ рдореЗрдВ рдПрдХ рдЫреЛрдЯреА рд╕рдореАрдХреНрд╖рд╛ рд▓рд┐рдЦрдиреЗ рдХрд╛ рдлреИрд╕рд▓рд╛ рдХрд┐рдпрд╛ (рдПрдбреЙрдкреНрдЯрд░ рднреА рд╡рд╣реАрдВ рдмрд┐рдХрддрд╛ рд╣реИ) рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд╢рд┐рдд рдХрд░рдиреЗ рдХреЗ рд▓рд┐рдП рдХреНрд╖рдорд╛ рдХрд░реЗрдВ рд╡рд┐рдлрд▓ рд░рд╣рд╛ред рдпрд╣ рдкрддрд╛ рдЪрд▓рддрд╛ рд╣реИ рдХрд┐ рдЕрдореЗрдЬрд╝реЕрди рдкрд░ рдПрдХ рдирд┐рдпрдо рд╣реИ: рдЖрдк рдХреЗрд╡рд▓ рддрднреА рд╕рдореАрдХреНрд╖рд╛ рдЬреЛрдбрд╝ рд╕рдХрддреЗ рд╣реИрдВ рдЬрдм рдЗрд╕ рд╕рд╛рдЗрдЯ рдкрд░ рд╡рд░реНрд╖ рдХреЗ рд▓рд┐рдП рдЦрд░реАрдж рдХреА рд░рд╛рд╢рд┐ рдХрдо рд╕реЗ рдХрдо $ 50 рд╣реЛред рдЗрд╕рд▓рд┐рдП, рдореИрдВ рдпрд╣рд╛рдВ рдПрдХ рд╕рдореАрдХреНрд╖рд╛ рдЫреЛрдбрд╝ рджреЗрддрд╛ рд╣реВрдВ, рдЬреЛ рдПрдбреЗрдкреНрдЯрд░ рдореЗрдВ рд░реБрдЪрд┐ рд░рдЦрддреЗ рд╣реИрдВ рдФрд░ рдЗрд╕реЗ рдЦрд░реАрджрдиреЗ рдХреА рдпреЛрдЬрдирд╛ рдмрдирд╛рддреЗ рд╣реИрдВред

USB - рдЕрдореЗрдЬрд╝рди рдкрд░ рд╕реАрдИрд╕реА рдПрдбрд╛рдкреНрдЯрд░ рдХреА рд╕рдореАрдХреНрд╖рд╛
I use this tiny (13g) adapter as reliable solution for the typical scenario. When PC starts up, the adapter powers on the TV, and switches the TV's input to HDMI1. When PC shuts down, the adapter powers the TV off.

All I had to do to make it work is to install the latest version of libCEC by Pulse-Eight on GitHub, and follow the instruction ┬лTurn on/off TV using USB-CEC Adapter (Windows Batch script)┬╗ published in FAQ section on Pulse-Eight web site.

The adapter also works in opposite way. If my PC is in sleep or hibernate state and I turn on my TV, the adapter wakes up the PC after 30 seconds, provided the HDMI1 source is selected on TV when it powers on. The same happens if I switch from watching TV to HDMI1 source (without 30 seconds delay). Don't know how to turn off this 'wake the PC' feature, though. By the way, when I power off the TV, the PC remains powered on.

My configuration:
ADAPTER тАФ firmware v9, libCEC v4.0.3, recognized in Windows Device Manager as ┬лPulse-Eight USB to HDMI CEC Adapter (rev.2)┬╗, and for unknown reason as ┬лHID-compliant mouse┬╗.
TV тАФ Samsung SmartTV LT27H390S (PC monitor with built-in TV-tuner), supports CEC v1.4.
PC тАФ Intel Core i5, Windows 10 x64 v1903.

The adapter supports CEC v1.4 (there is no difference between v1.4, v1.4a, and v1.4b in terms of CEC). It can emulate many CEC-types of devices: Recording, Playback, Tuner, Amplifier. It's even possible to emulate several types at once.

Hardware part is based on energy efficient AT90USB162 microcontroller. That's why the power consumption is less than 0.1W, and the box doesn't heat up.

Software part is based on Microsoft Visual C++ 2015 Redistributable Package (x86), and employs libusb-win32 when upgrading the firmware.

For those who experience any problems, here is a short troubleshooting list.
Ensure that the option ┬лAnynet+ (HDMI-CEC)┬╗ is on (located in TV Settings => General => External Device Manager).
HDMI cable that connects adapter to TV supports CEC.
For 'power on' feature to work, the adapter may have to be physically connected to HDMI 1 port (not HDMI 2, etc).
Update the firmware and software of your adapter.

I would definitely give this device 5 stars, but it has some considerable drawbacks:
As many users have already complained, there are no clear documentation, such as User Guide or at least step-by-step Quick Start Guide instruction in PDF form.
It seems like the development of libCEC has stopped. No new version has been released from November 2018 to January 2020.
Powering on the TV wakes up the PC if ┬лAllow this device to wake the computer┬╗ setting is cleared.
There are some functionality and usability issues with cec-client.exe and cec-tray.exe (both are part of libCEC software), but that's another storyтАж

Samsungctl.exe рдЙрдкрдпреЛрдЧрд┐рддрд╛ рдХрд╛ рдЙрдкрдпреЛрдЧ рдХрд░рдиреЗ рдХреА рдкреНрд░рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрд╛ рд╕рд░рд▓ рд╣реИ:

рд╕реЗрд╡рд╛ рдореЗрдиреВ (рдЙрдиреНрдирдд рдПрдХ рд╕рд╣рд┐рдд) рдХреИрд╕реЗ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдд рдХрд░реЗрдВ, рд╕рд╛рде рд╣реА рд╕рд╛рде рдЗрд╕рдХреЗ рдЕрдиреБрднрд╛рдЧреЛрдВ, рдорд╛рдкрджрдВрдбреЛрдВ рдФрд░ рдореВрд▓реНрдпреЛрдВ рдХрд╛ рд╡рд┐рд╡рд░рдг рдЗрд╕ рдкрд╛рда рдлрд╝рд╛рдЗрд▓ рдореЗрдВ рдкрд╛рдпрд╛ рдЬрд╛ рд╕рдХрддрд╛ рд╣реИ ред рд╕рдмрд╕реЗ рджрд┐рд▓рдЪрд╕реНрдк рдорд╛рдкрджрдВрдбреЛрдВ рд╕реЗ рдПрдХ рд╕рдВрдХреБрдЪрд┐рдд рдЕрдВрд╢ , рд╕реИрдордЬреАрдУ рдордВрдЪ рдкрд░ рдореЗрд░реА рдкреЛрд╕реНрдЯ рдореЗрдВ рдкрд╛рдпрд╛ рдЬрд╛ рд╕рдХрддрд╛ рд╣реИ ред

рд▓рдШреБрд░реВрдк
ATSC тАФ Advanced Television Systems Committee.

BLU тАФ BackLight Unit.

DDP тАФ Dolby Digital Plus.

DPMS тАФ Display Power Management Signaling (not supported on HDMI, as opposed to VGA and DVI).

EWBS тАФ Emergency Warning Broadcast System.

FRC тАФ Frame Rate Control.

IoT тАФ Internet of Things.

MICOM тАФ Microcontroller, responsible for receiving commands from an infrared remote control, switching main power supply on and off, resetting main SH4 CPU and so on. It also works as a watchdog.

MBR тАФ Multi-brand remote.

MRT тАФ Multiple Render Targets.

MVPD тАФ Multichannel Video Programming Distributors.

OCM тАФ Samsung One Connect Mini. Replaces built-in main board with external box.

OCF тАФ Open Connectivity Foundation, industrial IoT standard.

OOM тАФ Out-of-Memory.

OSD тАФ On Screen Display.

PDP тАФ Plasma Display Panel.

PVR тАФ Personal Video Recorder.

SPI тАФ Serial Peripheral Interface. Memory chip on the main board.

STB тАФ Set Top Box.

SWU тАФ Software Update.

T-CON тАФ Timing Controller (for LCD panel). Not present in Samsung T27H390.

WB тАФ White Balance.
